  (function(d) {
    function get_session_id() {
      function rand_4_char_str() {
        return Math.floor((1 + Math.random()) * 0x10000)
          .toString(16)
          .substring(1);
      }
      var session_id = '';
      // 80 character long session id
      for (var i = 0; i < 20; i++) {
        session_id += rand_4_char_str();
      }
      return session_id;
    }
    // Wrapped setItem() in a function due to empty block statement lint error
    function setSessionIdToLocalStorage(tagsSessionId) {
      try {
        localStorage.setItem('tags_session_id', tagsSessionId);
      } catch (err) { // Safari private browsing mode fix.
        return false;
      }
    }

    window.tags_session_id = localStorage.getItem('tags_session_id');
    if (window.tags_session_id === null) {
      window.tags_session_id = get_session_id();
      setSessionIdToLocalStorage(window.tags_session_id);
    }

    function fnProject_tablegetJobTypes(oObj) {
        var jobIds = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.jobs].split(',');
        var jobLinks = new Array();
        jq.each(jobIds, function(index, value) {
            if (jobInfo[value]) {
                var jobDetails = jobInfo[value];
                jobLinks.push('<a class="hiddenlink" href="https://www.freelancer.pk/jobs/' + jobDetails.seo_url + '/">' + jobDetails.name + '</a>');
            }
        });
        return jobLinks.join(', ');
    }
    

    
    function redrawProject_table(m, callback) {
        jq('#project_table' + '_processing').css('display', '');
        jq('#project_table_wrapper .ns_refresh').addClass('ns_refreshing');
        project_table_cache.haData.clear();

        if (m === true) {
            project_table_m = true;
        }
        jq('#project_table').dataTable().fnDraw();
        if (typeof callback == 'function') {
            project_table_drawCallback = callback;
        }

        if (typeof window.browseProjectLib == 'object') {
            var table_height = jq('#project_table').height();
            jq('#project_table' + '_processing').css('padding-top', table_height * 0.2 +
                'px').height(table_height * 0.8 + 'px');
        }
    }

    function fnProject_tableDataTablesPipeline(sSource, aoData, fnCallback) {
        

        var iPipe = 5;
        var bNeedServer = false;
        var sEcho = fnGetKey(aoData, 'sEcho');
        var iRequestStart = fnGetKey(aoData, 'iDisplayStart');
        var iRequestLength = fnGetKey(aoData, 'iDisplayLength');
        var iRequestEnd = iRequestStart + iRequestLength;
        project_table_cache.iDisplayStart = iRequestStart;

        if (iRequestEnd > project_table_cache.iTotalDisplayRecords) {
            iRequestEnd = project_table_cache.iTotalDisplayRecords;
        }
        if (project_table_cache.haData.items.length == 0 || !project_table_cache.haData.hasRangeOfItems(iRequestStart, iRequestEnd) || project_table_m === true) {
            bNeedServer = true;
        }

        if (window.searchOptions) {
            var additionalVars = window.searchOptions.convertToArray();
            jQuery.merge(aoData, additionalVars);
            projectSkills = {};

            if (!prefillOptions || (prefillOptions && prefillOptions.pushStateRoot != '/jobs/ending')) {
                if (fnGetKey(aoData, 'iSortCol_0') == 6 && fnGetKey(aoData, 'sSortDir_0') == 'asc') {
                    fnSetKey(aoData, 'iSortCol_0', 8);
                    fnSetKey(aoData, 'sSortDir_0', 'asc');
                    window['project_table_hideCol'] = 'started-col';
                    jq('th.started-col').removeClass('sorting_asc');
                    jq('th.started-col').removeClass('sorting_desc');
                    jq('th.end-col').addClass('sorting_asc');
                    bNeedServer = true;
                } else if (fnGetKey(aoData, 'iSortCol_0') == 8) {
                    fnSetKey(aoData, 'iSortCol_0', 6);
                    fnSetKey(aoData, 'sSortDir_0', 'desc');
                    window['project_table_hideCol'] = 'end-col';
                    jq('th.end-col').removeClass('sorting_asc');
                    jq('th.end-col').removeClass('sorting_desc');
                    jq('th.started-col').addClass('sorting_desc');
                    bNeedServer = true;
                }
            }
        }

        // for #full_invitation_table on inviteFriends.php
        if (window.referrals_filter) {
            jQuery.merge(aoData, {referrals_filter:window.referrals_filter});
        }

        // Has sorting changed?
        if (project_table_cache.lastRequest && !bNeedServer) {
            for (var i = 0, iLen = Math.min(aoData.length, project_table_cache.lastRequest.length); i < iLen; ++i) {
                if (aoData[i].name != 'iDisplayStart' && aoData[i].name != 'iDisplayLength' && aoData[i].name != 'sEcho') {
                    if (aoData[i].value != project_table_cache.lastRequest[i].value) {
                        bNeedServer = true;
                        project_table_cache.haData.clear();
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        
        /**
         * Target ads on the page according to the DataTable criteria.
         *
         * @param  {Object} targeting The ad targeting criteria. If undefined, then the criteria are read from the DataTable cache.
         * @return {void}
         */
        var retargetAds = function(targeting) {
            var ads = project_table_cache.ads || {};
            var previous = null;

            if (!ads.init) {
                ads.init = true;
                ads.targeting = targeting || ads.targeting;

                /**
                 * The initial ad targeting is set outside of the DataTable, so
                 * that it doesn't need to wait for the DataTable to load.
                 */
                return;
            } else {
                previous = ads.targeting;
                ads.targeting = targeting || ads.targeting;
            }

            if (JSON.stringify(previous) !== JSON.stringify(ads.targeting)) {
                window._adq = window._adq || [];
                window._adq.push(
                    ['_setProperties', ads.targeting],
                    '_refresh'
                );
            }
        };
        

        // Store the request for checking next time
        project_table_cache.lastRequest = aoData.slice();
        if (bNeedServer) {
            jq('#project_table').css('opacity', 0.7);

            if (iRequestStart < project_table_cache.iCacheLower) {
                iRequestStart = iRequestStart - (iRequestLength * (iPipe - 1));
                if (iRequestStart < 0) {
                    iRequestStart = 0;
                }
            }

            project_table_cache.iCacheLower = iRequestStart;
            project_table_cache.iCacheUpper = iRequestStart + (iRequestLength * iPipe);
            project_table_cache.iDisplayLength = fnGetKey(aoData, 'iDisplayLength');
            fnSetKey(aoData, 'iDisplayStart', iRequestStart);
            fnSetKey(aoData, 'iDisplayLength', iRequestLength * iPipe);
            jq.merge(aoData, getExtraProject_tableValuesToSend());
            
            if (project_table_m === true) {
                aoData.push({'name': 'm', 'value': true});
                project_table_m = false;
            }

            if (fnGetKey(aoData, 'currency') == 'bonus') {
                var bonus = {'name': 'bonus', 'value': true};
                aoData.push(bonus);
            }
            
            
            jq.ajax({
                "dataType": 'json',
                "type": "POST",
                "url": sSource,
                "data": aoData,
                "success": function(json, aoData) {
                    for (var i = project_table_cache.iCacheLower; i < project_table_cache.iCacheUpper; ++i) {
                        project_table_cache.haData.setItem(i, json.aaData[i - project_table_cache.iCacheLower]);
                    }
                    project_table_cache.iTotalRecords = json.iTotalRecords;
                    project_table_cache.iTotalDisplayRecords = json.iTotalDisplayRecords;

                    // Prepare requested json from server's json
                    if (project_table_cache.iCacheLower != project_table_cache.iDsiplayStart) {
                        json.aaData.splice(0, project_table_cache.iDisplayStart - project_table_cache.iCacheLower);
                    }
                    json.aaData.splice(project_table_cache.iDisplayLength, json.aaData.length);

                    
                    // Ad targeting
                    retargetAds(json.adTargeting);
                    delete json.adTargeting;
                    
                    fnCallback(json);
                }
            });
            
        } else {
            // Prepare json from hash
            var json = {};
            json.sEcho = sEcho;
            json.iTotalRecords = project_table_cache.iTotalRecords;
            json.iTotalDisplayRecords = project_table_cache.iTotalDisplayRecords;
            json.aaData = [];
            for (var i = iRequestStart; i < iRequestEnd; ++i) {
                json.aaData[i - iRequestStart] = project_table_cache.haData.getItem(i);
            }

            
            // Ad targeting
            retargetAds();
            

            fnCallback(json);
            return;
        }
    }

    function fnGetKey(aoData, sKey) {
        for (var i = 0, iLen = aoData.length; i < iLen; i++) {
            if (aoData[i].name == sKey) {
                return aoData[i].value;
            }
        }
        return null;
    }

    function fnSetKey(aoData, sKey, mValue) {
        for (var i = 0, iLen = aoData.length; i < iLen; i++) {
            if (aoData[i].name == sKey) {
                aoData[i].value = mValue;
            }
        }
    }

    function isInView(selector) {
        var docViewTop = jq(window).scrollTop();
        var docViewBottom = docViewTop + jq(window).height();
        var elemTop = jq(selector).offset().top;
        return ((elemTop >= docViewTop) && (elemTop <= docViewBottom));
    }

    function Hash() {
        this.length = 0;
        this.items = new Array();

        for (var i = 0; i < arguments.length; i += 2) {
            if (typeof(arguments[i + 1]) != 'undefined') {
                this.items[arguments[i]] = arguments[i + 1];
                this.length++;
            }
        }

        this.removeItem = function(key) {
            var tmp_previous;
            if (typeof(this.items[key]) != 'undefined') {
                this.length--;
                var tmp_previous = this.items[key];
                delete this.items[key];
            }

            return tmp_previous;
        }

        this.getItem = function(key) {
            return this.items[key];
        }

        this.setItem = function(key, value) {
            var tmp_previous;
            if (typeof(value) != 'undefined') {
                if (typeof(this.items[key]) == 'undefined') {
                    this.length++;
                } else {
                    tmp_previous = this.items[key];
                }

                this.items[key] = value;
            }

            return tmp_previous;
        }

        this.hasItem = function(key) {
            return typeof(this.items[key]) != 'undefined';
        }

        this.hasRangeOfItems = function(begin, end) {
            for (var i = begin; i < end; ++i) {
                if (!this.hasItem(i)) {
                    return false;
                }
            }
            return true;
        }

        this.clear = function() {
            for (var i in this.items) {
                delete this.items[i];
            }
            this.items = new Array();

            this.length = 0;
        }
    }

    function fnProject_tableOneTimeCallback() {
        if (typeof project_table_drawCallback == 'function') {
            project_table_drawCallback();
            project_table_drawCallback = undefined;
        }
    }
</script>

    var CONTEST_TYPE = 'c';

    function setInfowindowData (data, index) {
        var infowindow = {};
        infowindow.lat = data[index.lat];
        infowindow.lon = data[index.lon];
        if (!infowindow.lat || !infowindow.lon) {
            return;
        }
        infowindow.name = data[index.name];
        infowindow.budget = data[index.budget];
        infowindow.seo_url = data[index.seo_url];
        infowindow.location = [];
        if (data[index.vicinity]) {
            infowindow.location.push(data[index.vicinity]);
        }
        if (data[index.administrative_area_level_1]) {
            infowindow.location.push(data[index.administrative_area_level_1]);
        }
        if (data[index.project_country]) {
            infowindow.location.push(data[index.project_country]);
        }
        infowindow.address = infowindow.location.join(', ');
        infowindow.hourly = data[index.duration] != 'Fixed';
        infowindowData.push(infowindow);
    }

    function fnProject_tableStartRender(oObj) {

        var contestExtendedLabel = '';
        if (contestExtended) {
            contestExtendedLabel = "<span class='status-label is-large is-urgent'>Extended</span>";

    }

    function fnProject_tableLeftRender(oObj) {
        var contestExtended = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.extended] == 1 ? true : false;
        var contestExtendedLabel = '';
        if (contestExtended) {
            contestExtendedLabel = "<span class='status-label is-large is-urgent'>Extended</span>";

    }

    function fnProject_tableAvgRender(oObj) {
        var price;
        var priceDetails;
        if (oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.type] == PROJECT_TYPE) {
            if (oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.duration] == 'Fixed') {
                var bids = jq(oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.bids]).data('bids');
                if (typeof bids == 'undefined' || bids == 0 || oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.sealed] == true) {
                    price = processProjectBudget(oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.budget], 'fixed');
                } else {
                    price = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.avg];
                }
            } else {
                if ((oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.avg] == '') || (oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.avg] == '-')) {
                    price = processProjectBudget(oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.budget], 'hourly') + " <small>" + oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.duration] + "</small>";
                } else {
                    price = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.avg] + " " + "\/ hr" + "<small>" + oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.duration] + '</small>';
                }
            }

            priceDetails = '<span class="average-bid">' + price + '</span>' +
                ( ((verifiedRender(oObj) || xpbonusRender(oObj)) && !minimalRows) ? '<div class="ProjectTable-status">' + verifiedRender(oObj) + xpbonusRender(oObj) + '</div>': '') +
                '<div class="ProjectTable-controls"></div>';

        } else if (oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.type] == CONTEST_TYPE) {
            priceDetails = '<span class="average-bid">' + oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.avg] + '</span>' +
                ((oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.guaranteed] == true && !minimalRows) ?  '<div class="ProjectTable-status"><span class="status-label is-large is-success" ' +
                    'data-toggle="popover" data-placement="left" ' +
                    'data-content="Guaranteed contests ensure a winner to be chosen and awarded the prize.">Guaranteed</span></div>' : '') +
                verifiedRender(oObj) + '<div class="ProjectTable-controls"></div>';
        }
        return priceDetails;
    }

    function fnProject_tableJobsRender(oObj) {

        var jobIds = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.jobs].split(',');
        var projectId = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.id];
        //save project skills as it will be overridden
        projectSkills[projectId] = jobIds;
        var xpbonus = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.xpbonus];
        if (!(xpbonus && jq(jobIds).is([]))) {
            oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.xpbonus] = '';
        }

        return Project_tablegetProjectsAndContestsJobTypes(oObj);
    }

    function fnProject_tableWatchRender(oObj) {
        var tooltipMessage,
            id = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.id],
            type = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.type],
            bookmarked = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.watch],
            bookmark = jq('<a>').attr({
                'class': 'bookmark',
                'data-project-id': id,
                'data-type': type
            }),
            bookmarkType = type == 'p' ? 'project' : 'contest',
            bookmarkMsg = bookmarked ? 'unbookmark' : 'bookmark';

        if (bookmarked) {
            bookmark.addClass('selected');
            bookmark.attr('data-action', 'off');
        } else {
            bookmark.attr('data-action', 'on');
        }

        tooltipMessage = bookmarkTooltipMsg[bookmarkType][bookmarkMsg];
        var bookmarkSvg = jq('#flicon-bookmark').text();
        bookmark.append(jq('<div class="bookmark-inner">' +
            '<span data-toggle="popover" href="javascript:void(0)" data-placement="left" data-content="' + tooltipMessage + '">' + bookmarkSvg +
            '</span></div>'));
        return jq('<div>').append(bookmark).html();
    }

    function skillsRender(oObj) {
        var jobIds = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.jobs].split(',');
        var jobLinks = new Array();
        jq.each(jobIds, function(index, value) {
            if (jobInfo[value]) {
                var jobDetails = jobInfo[value];
                if (!bookmarkClickOnly) {
                    jobLinks.push('<a class="hiddenlink" href="https://www.freelancer.pk/jobs/' + jobDetails.seo_url + '/">' + jobDetails.name + '</a>');
                } else {
                    jobLinks.push('<span class="PageBookmarkOnboarding-project-skills">' + jobDetails.name + '</span>');
                }
            }
        });
        return jobLinks.join(', ');
    }

    function verifiedRender(oObj) {
        var verified = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.isPaymentVerified];
        if (verified !== '1') {
            return '';
        } else {
            var tickSvg = jq('#flicon-tick').text();
            return '<span class="status-label is-large is-success" ' +
                          'data-toggle="popover" data-placement="left" ' +
                          'data-content="Employer has a verified payment method">'
                          + currencyCodeSign.sign + tickSvg +
                    '</span>';
        }
    }

    function xpbonusRender(oObj) {
        var xpbonus = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.xpbonus];
        if (!xpbonus) {
            return '';
        } else {
            return '<span class="status-label is-large is-success" ' +
                        'xpbonus="' + xpbonus + '" data-toggle="popover" data-placement="left" ' +
                        'data-content="Earn extra XP when placing a bid on this project">+ ' +
                        xpbonus + ' XP' +
                    '</span>';
        }
    }

    function fnProject_tableRowCallback(nRow, aData, iDisplayIndex) {
        // Enable bid checking on the row
        jq(nRow).attr("project_id", aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.id]);
        jq(nRow).attr("bid_placed_check",1);

        jq(nRow).addClass('ProjectTable-row project-details');
        jq(nRow).attr('id', aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.id]);

        //Highlight the row for Highlight Contests
        if (aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.highlight] == "true" && !minimalRows) {
            jq(nRow).addClass('highlight-contest');
        }

        // Highlight rows that are in the bookmarks section at the top of the table.
        if (aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.bookmarkSection] == "true") {
            jq(nRow).addClass('highlight-bookmark');
        }

        // Finds bookmarked jobs and highlight them in main table section (for onboarding table)
        if (jq(nRow).find("a.bookmark").hasClass('selected') && highlightBookmarks) {
            jq(nRow).addClass('highlight-bookmark');
        }

        var privateFlag = aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.private];

        generateRepostLink(nRow, aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.id],
            privateFlag, aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.type], aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.jobs]);

        return nRow;
    }

    function processProjectBudget(budgetObject, type) {
        var min = budgetObject.minbudget_usd / exchangeRate;
        var max = budgetObject.maxbudget_usd / exchangeRate;

        if (typeof max != 'undefined' && max != '') {
            var budget = currencyCodeSign.sign +
                            Math.floor(min) +
                            ' - ' + currencyCodeSign.sign +
                            Math.ceil(max) +
                            (type == 'hourly' ? T_('/hr') : '');
            return budget;
        } else {
            var budget = currencyCodeSign.sign + Math.floor(min) + '+';
            return budget;
        }
    }

    function generateRepostLink(nRow, project_id, privateFlag, type, projectSKills) {
        var freelancerAccount = (typeof isFreelancer != 'undefined') ? isFreelancer : false;
        if (type == 'c') { //if it it is a contest
            var repostButtonLabel = 'Post a contest like this';
        } else {  //for other situations
            var repostButtonLabel = 'Post a project like this';
        }

        //check the eligibility of Bid Now button
        var requiredSkills = projectSkills[project_id];
        var eligible = false;

        for (index in requiredSkills) {
            var val = requiredSkills[index];
            if(typeof seller_jobs['s' + val] != 'undefined') {
                eligible = true;
                break;
            }
        }

        // If user is in /jobs/localjobs always show Bid Button
        if (window.localJobs) {
            eligible = true;
        }

        if (!minimalRows) {
            var projectDescrTemplate = _.template(window.descr_tmpl, {
                projectId: project_id,
                type: type,
                buttonLabel: repostButtonLabel,
                eligible : eligible,
                isPrivate: privateFlag,
                SSL_BASE_URL: 'https://www.freelancer.pk',
                isFreelancer: freelancerAccount,
                
                
            });
            jq(nRow).find('.ProjectTable-controls').html(projectDescrTemplate);
        }
    }

    function fnProject_tableDrawCallback() {
        if (infowindowData.length > 0) {
            jq.each(infowindowData, function(i, data) {
                jq('#project-map-canvas').trigger('add', [data]);
            });
            infowindowData = [];
        }
        

        //get the pagination marked
        jq('#project_table_paginate span:nth-child(3) span').each(function() {
            jq(this).attr('id', 'paginiate_bottom_' + jq(this).text());
        });
        //update the first and last page number for table
        window.pagination_start = jq('.table_paginate.paginate_button.number').first().text();
        window.pagination_last = jq('.table_paginate.paginate_button.number').last().text();

        //insert the custom pagination template
        var paginationControlVars = {
            start: parseInt(window.pagination_start),
            last : parseInt(window.pagination_last)

        };
        var $paginationControl = jq('#browse-projects-pagination');
        if (typeof projectPagintorUrlValues !== 'undefined') {
            paginationControlVars['urlBase'] = projectPagintorUrlValues['urlBase'];
            paginationControlVars['urlPreNumber'] = projectPagintorUrlValues['urlPreNumber'];
            paginationControlVars['currentPageNum'] = 0;
            paginationControlVars['lastPageNum'] = 0;
            if (projectPagintorUrlValues['currentPageNum']) {
                paginationControlVars['currentPageNum'] = projectPagintorUrlValues['currentPageNum'];
            }
            if (projectPagintorUrlValues['lastPageNum']) {
                paginationControlVars['lastPageNum'] = projectPagintorUrlValues['lastPageNum'];
            }
        }
        $paginationControl.html(_.template(window.pagination_tmpl, paginationControlVars));

        //remove the original pagniation template
        jq('#project_table_length').remove();

        if (window.browseProjectLib) {
            window.browseProjectLib.descriptionTransition.init(jq('#project_table'));

            //hide pagination when no pages or 1 page only, and highlight active page
            if (window.pagination_last <= 1) { //hide the show X entries control
                jq('.project-table-length').hide();
            } else {
                var pg = jq('#project_table_info').next('.pagination').find('.active.number.paginate_button a').text();

                jq('#pagination_top_' +pg).addClass('paginate_active');
                jq('.project-table-length').show();
                //disable the prev and first button when on first page
                if (pg == '1') {
                    jq('#pagination_top_first').addClass('disabled');
                    jq('#pagination_top_prev').addClass('disabled');
                } else if (jq('#pagination_top_' +pg).parent().next().find('#pagination_top_next').length > 0) {
                    //if this is the last page.
                    //
                    jq('#pagination_top_next').addClass('disabled');
                    jq('#pagination_top_last').addClass('disabled');
                }

                
                
                if (typeof history.pushState == 'function') {
                    //detect and remove existing pagination in url
                    var pathArray = window.location.pathname.split('/');
                    //when the last chaaracter of pathname is '/', the last element
                    //in array will be empty, thus in this case, the last element
                    //shall be directed to the last but 2 element.
                    var lastIndex = (pathArray[pathArray.length - 1] == '' && pathArray.length - 1 > 0) ? pathArray.length - 2 : pathArray.length - 1;
                    if (jq.isNumeric(pathArray[lastIndex])) {
                        pathArray = pathArray.splice(0, lastIndex);
                        pathArray.push('');
                    }
                    var path = pathArray.join('/');
                    var url = path + pg + '/' + window.location.search + window.location.hash;
                    if (pg === '1' && pathArray.length === 4 && jq.inArray(pathArray[1], ['jobs', 'work', 'job-search']) !== -1) {
                        url = path + window.location.search + window.location.hash;
                    }
                    if (window.justLoaded) {
                        history.replaceState('', document.title, url);
                        window.justLoaded = false;
                    } else {
                        history.pushState('', document.title, url);
                    }
                }
                
                
            }

            // comment out for now, TO BE REMOVED WHEN CONFIRMED
            // jq('#tableResultCount').text(jq('#project_table').dataTable().fnSettings()._iRecordsTotal);
            if (!prefillOptions || (prefillOptions && prefillOptions.pushStateRoot != "/jobs/ending")) {
                if (window['project_table_hideCol'] == 'started-col') {
                    jq('#project_table th.started-col').removeClass('sorting_asc');
                    jq('#project_table th.started-col').removeClass('sorting_desc');
                    if (window['project_table_addSortingClass'] == true) {
                        jq('#project_table th.end-col').addClass('sorting_asc');
                    }
                    jq('#project_table .started-col').hide();
                    jq('#project_table .end-col').show();
                } else if (window['project_table_hideCol'] == 'end-col') {
                    jq('#project_table th.end-col').removeClass('sorting_asc');
                    jq('#project_table th.end-col').removeClass('sorting_desc');
                    if (window['project_table_addSortingClass'] == true) {
                        jq('#project_table th.started-col').addClass('sorting_desc');
                    }
                    jq('#project_table .end-col').hide();
                    jq('#project_table .started-col').show();
                } else {
                    jq('#project_table .end-col').hide();
                    jq('#project_table .started-col').show();
                    if (window['project_table_addSortingClass'] == false) {
                        jq('#project_table .end-col').removeClass('sorting_asc').addClass('sorting');
                        jq('#project_table .started-col').removeClass('sorting_desc').addClass('sorting');
                    }
                }
                window['project_table_addSortingClass'] = true;
            }
        } else {
            jq('#project_table .end-col').hide();
            jq('#project_table .started-col').show();
        }
        if (jq('#project_table_info').next().find('li').length <= 5) {
            jq('.dataTables_paginate').hide();
        } else {
            jq('.dataTables_paginate').show();
        }

        // Shows the end-col th when table is empty to fix the broken layout cause by DataTable
        if (jq('#project_table').find('.dataTables_empty').length) {
            jq('#project_table th.started-col').removeClass('sorting_desc');
            jq('#project_table .end-col').show();
        }
        jq('#project_table' + '_processing').css('display', 'none');
    }

    function fnProject_tableOneTimeCallback() {
        // linksTemplate should only be defined for VariantX abtest
        if (jq('#table-footer').length) {
            jq('#browse-project-table tr:last').after(jq('#table-footer').html());

        jq('.contest_tab').html('Contests');
        jq('.xpbonus_tab').html('<span class=\u0022ns_bubble-xp\u0022>+ XP<\/span> Projects');
    }

    function Project_tablegetProjectsAndContestsJobTypes(oObj) {
        var jobIds = oObj.aData[project_tableColumnIndexes.jobs].split(',');
        var jobLinks = new Array();
        jq.each(jobIds, function(index, value) {
            if (jobInfo[value]) {
                var jobDetails = jobInfo[value];
                jobLinks.push('<a class="hiddenlink" href="https://www.freelancer.pk/jobs/' + jobDetails.seo_url + '/">' + jobDetails.name + '</a>');
            }
        });
        return jobLinks.join('');
    }

    function getExtraProject_tableValuesToSend() {
        jq('#project-map-canvas').trigger('clear');

        //load extra values if it is minimized version, these values are

                   "value": []});
        
        
            vals.push({"name": "jobIdEnable", "value": "on"});
        

        
            vals.push({"name": "status", "value": "open"});
        
        

        return vals;
    }

    jq(document).ready(function() {

        jq(document).ready(function() {

            
            
                window['project_table_addSortingClass'] = true;
            

            window.justLoaded = true;

            jq('.project_tab').live('click', function() {
                jq('#contest_table_tab').hide();
                jq('#xpbonus_table_tab').hide();
                jq('#project_table_tab').show();

            jq('.contest_tab').live('click', function() {
                jq('#project_table_tab').hide();
                jq('#xpbonus_table_tab').hide();
                jq('#contest_table_tab').show();
            });

            jq('.xpbonus_tab').live('click', function() {
                jq('#contest_table_tab').hide();
                jq('#project_table_tab').hide();
                jq('#xpbonus_table_tab').show();
                jq('.project_tab').html('Projects');
                jq('.contest_tab').html('Contests');
                jq('.xpbonus_tab').html('<span class=\u0022ns_bubble-xp\u0022>+ XP<\/span> Projects');
            });
        });

        //watch project
        if (bookmarkClickOnly) {
            jq('#project_table.dataTable').on('click', '.ProjectTable-row', function () {
                watchProject.call(jq(this).find('.bookmark-inner'));
            });
        } else {
            jq('#project_table.dataTable').on('click', '.bookmark-inner', watchProject);
        }

        function watchProject() {
            var that = this,
                action = jq(this).parent().attr('data-action'),
                $bookmark = jq('span.fl-icon-star-full', this),
                type = jq(this).parent().data('type') === 'c' ? 'c' : 'p',
                project_id = jq(this).parent().data('project-id');

            jq.ajax({
                url: '/projects/watch-universal.php',
                type: 'GET',
                data: {
                    'project_id' : project_id,
                    'action' : action,
                    'type' : type
                },
                dataType: 'json',
                cache: false,
                timeout: 10000,
                tryCount: 0,
                retryLimit: 5,
                success: function(msg) {
                    if (msg == null) {
                        showError(that, T_('Oops! There seems to be a server problem, please try again later.'));
                    } else if (msg['status'] != 'success') {
                        showError(that, msg['errors']);
                    } else {
                        var bookmarkType = type == 'p' ? 'project' : 'contest',
                            bookmarkMsg = action == 'on' ? 'unbookmark' : 'bookmark',
                            trackingAction = action == 'on' ? 'bookmark' : 'unbookmark',
                            dataAction = action == 'on' ? 'off' : 'on';

                        jq(that).parent().attr('data-action', dataAction);
                        $bookmark.attr('data-content', bookmarkTooltipMsg[bookmarkType][bookmarkMsg]);
                        if (highlightBookmarks) {
                            jq(that).closest("tr").toggleClass("highlight-bookmark");
                        }

                        // This is to check we are on the onboarding funnel version of the page.
                        if (bookmarkClickOnly && dataAction === 'off' && msg['watch_count'] >= 10) {
                            // Check if user has 10 bookmarks, and if so, get them to continue through the funnel.
                            jq('#project_table_info').hide();
                            jq('.dataTables_paginate').hide();
                            jq('#browse-project-table-overlay').css("display", "flex").hide().fadeIn(600);
                        }
                    }
                },
                error: function(xhr, textStatus, errorThrown) {
                    if ((textStatus == 'timeout') || (xhr.status == 502)) {
                        this.tryCount++;
                        if (this.tryCount <= this.retryLimit) {
                            //try again
                            jq.ajax(this);
                            return;
                        }
                        showError(that, T_('Seem we lost connection to server somehow'));
                    }
                    if (xhr.status == 500) {
                        showError(that, T_('Oops! There seems to be a server problem, please try again later.'));
                    } else {
                        showError(that, T_('Oops! There was a problem, sorry.'));
                    }
                    //bookmarkFail(action, that);
                }
            });
        }

        function showError(that, errors) {
            var offset = jQuery(that).offset();
            var y = parseInt(offset.top);
            var x = parseInt(offset.left);
            var msg = '';
            if (errors instanceof Array) {
                jQuery.each(errors, function(index, error) {
                    msg += (index == 0 ? '' : '<br>') + error;
                });
            } else {
                msg = errors;
            }
            var bookmarkErrorTemplate = _.template(window.bookmark_tmpl, {
                msg: msg
            });
            var that = jQuery(bookmarkErrorTemplate)
                .insertAfter(that).offset({top: y - 10, left: x - 247});
            setTimeout(function() {
                jQuery(that).fadeOut(1000, function() {
                    jQuery(this).remove();
                });
            }, 3000);
            // enable click on popover
            that.find('a').click(
                function(e){
                    window.location.href=jQuery(e.target).closest('a').attr('href');
                }
            )
        }
    });
</script>

    function loadGARemarketingPixel(usertype) {
        if (!document.getElementById('remarketingPixel')) {
            var google_tag_params = google_tag_params || {};
            var trackUrl = "https://www.googleadservices.com/pagead/conversion/viewthroughconversion/1015002772/";
            var params =  "?value=0&guid=ON&script=0&remarketing_only=true";
            params = params + '&usertype=' + usertype;
            var img = document.createElement("img");
            img.id = 'remarketingPixel'
            img.src = trackUrl + params;
            document.body.appendChild(img);
        }
    }
</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
(function() {
    function hiremeTrack(e) {
        if (window.allowHireMeTracking === true || window.allowHireMeTracking === undefined) {
            var source = jQuery(e.target).attr('hireme-source'),
                event = jQuery(e.target).attr('hireme-event');
                label = jQuery(e.target).attr('hireme-label');

            if (source || event) {
                window.allowHireMeTracking = false;
            }

            if (source) {
                window._ttref.push(
                    ['_clearEntrypoint', 'ProjectHireMe'],
                    ['_setCookie', 'ProjectHireMe_' + source]);
            }

            if (event) {
                var data = ['_trackEvent', 'ProjectHireMe', event];
                if (label) {
                    data.push(label);
                }
                window._ttref.push(data);
            }

            setTimeout(function() { window.allowHireMeTracking = true; }, 100);
        }
    }

    jQuery(document).ready(function() {
        var selector = '[hireme-source],[hireme-event]',
            observer,
            MutationObserver = window.MutationObserver ||
                window.WebKitMutationObserver ||
                window.MozMutationObserver;

        if (MutationObserver !== undefined) {
            jQuery(selector).on('mousedown', hiremeTrack);

            observer = new MutationObserver(function() {
                jQuery(selector).off('mousedown', hiremeTrack);
                jQuery(selector).on('mousedown', hiremeTrack);
            });

            observer.observe(document.body, {
                childList: true,
                subtree: true
            });
        }
    });

})();
</script>
